# Task: Design a Priority-Based Shard Allocation Strategy

## Background
Elasticsearch's shard allocation balances shards across nodes, but doesn't support priority-based allocation where critical indices get preferred placement on faster nodes.

## Objective
Design a new `PriorityShardsAllocator` that extends the existing allocation framework to support index-priority-aware shard placement.

## Steps
1. Study the existing shard allocation in `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/`
2. Understand the `ShardsAllocator` interface and `BalancedShardsAllocator`
3. Study `AllocationDeciders` and how decisions compose
4. Create a design document `design_doc.md` in `/workspace/` with:
   - Architecture overview of current allocation
   - Proposed PriorityShardsAllocator class design
   - New `AllocationDecider` for priority constraints
   - Index setting for priority level (`index.routing.allocation.priority`)
   - Interaction with existing deciders (DiskThresholdDecider, AwarenessAllocationDecider)
   - API changes needed
5. Create a skeleton Java file `PriorityShardsAllocator.java` showing the class structure

## Key Reference Files
- `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/allocator/BalancedShardsAllocator.java`
- `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/allocator/ShardsAllocator.java`
- `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/decider/AllocationDeciders.java`

## Success Criteria
- Design doc exists with architecture overview
- Skeleton Java file exists
- Design references existing allocation classes
- Includes interaction with existing deciders

Perfect! Here's a summary of what I've delivered:

## ✅ Priority-Based Shard Allocation Design - Complete

I've successfully designed a comprehensive **priority-based shard allocation strategy** for Elasticsearch v8.17.0 with **2,176 lines** of design documentation and skeleton code across 5 files.

---

## 📦 Deliverables

### 1. **design_doc.md** (587 lines)
A comprehensive design specification covering:
- **Current architecture**: Detailed analysis of ShardsAllocator, BalancedShardsAllocator, and AllocationDeciders
- **Problem statement**: Why priority-aware allocation is needed
- **Proposed design**: Four components:
  - `index.routing.allocation.priority` setting (0-100 scale)
  - `node.attr.allocation_tier` classification (e.g., "premium", "standard")
  - `PriorityAllocationDecider` - enforces priority constraints
  - `PriorityShardsAllocator` - reorders shards for priority-first allocation
- **Integration with existing deciders**: DiskThresholdDecider, AwarenessAllocationDecider, etc.
- **API specification**: All new cluster and index settings
- **Behavior examples**: 3 real-world scenarios with expected outcomes
- **Testing strategy**, **backward compatibility**, **performance analysis**, and **security considerations**

### 2. **PriorityShardsAllocator.java** (448 lines)
Complete skeleton implementing `ShardsAllocator` interface:
- Wraps `BalancedShardsAllocator` via decorator pattern
- Reorders unassigned shards by index priority (highest first)
- Dynamic configuration via `ClusterSettings`
- Comprehensive JavaDoc and error handling
- Configuration methods for testing

### 3. **PriorityAllocationDecider.java** (458 lines)
Complete skeleton extending `AllocationDecider`:
- Decision logic: YES/THROTTLE based on priority and node tier
- High-priority shards prefer
... (truncated)

  "content": "# Priority-Based Shard Allocation Strategy Design\n\n## Executive Summary\n\nThis document describes the design of a new `PriorityShardsAllocator` component for Elasticsearch that extends the existing shard allocation framework to support **priority-aware allocation**. The allocator enables critical indices to be preferentially placed on faster (higher-capacity or better-performing) nodes within the cluster.\n\n---\n\n## 1. Current Architecture Overview\n\n### 1.1 Existing Allocation Framework\n\nElasticsearch's shard allocation is based on a **pluggable architecture** with three core components:\n\n#### **ShardsAllocator Interface**\n- **Location**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/allocator/ShardsAllocator.java`\n- **Responsibilities**:\n  - `allocate(RoutingAllocation)` - Main allocation method\n  - `allocate(RoutingAllocation, ActionListener<Void>)` - Async variant\n  - `decideShardAllocation(ShardRouting, RoutingAllocation)` - Explain API support\n  - `execute(RoutingAllocation, AllocationCommands, ...)` - Execute explicit commands\n\n#### **BalancedShardsAllocator**\n- **Location**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/allocator/BalancedShardsAllocator.java`\n- **Current Implementation**: Balances shards using weighted function approach\n- **Balance Factors**:\n  - Shard count balance (cluster.routing.allocation.balance.shard)\n  - Index spread balance (cluster.routing.allocation.balance.index)\n  - Write load balance (cluster.routing.allocation.balance.write_load)\n  - Disk usage balance (cluster.routing.allocation.balance.disk_usage)\n- **Design Pattern**: Uses WeightFunction to compute node scores; allocates to node with highest score\n\n#### **AllocationDeciders Composition**\n- **Location**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/decider/AllocationDeciders.java`\n- **Purpose**: Combines multiple AllocationDecider instances using **fail-fast AND logic**\n  - Returns YES (proceed), THROTTLE (rate-limit), or NO (reject)\n  - First NO result blocks allocation\n- **Methods**:\n  - `canAllocate(ShardRouting, RoutingNode, RoutingAllocation)`\n  - `canRebalance(ShardRouting, RoutingAllocation)`\n  - `canRemain(ShardRouting, RoutingNode, RoutingAllocation)`\n  - `shouldAutoExpandToNode(IndexMetadata, DiscoveryNode, RoutingAllocation)`\n\n#### **AllocationDecider Base Class**\n- **Location**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/decider/AllocationDecider.java`\n- **Design**: Abstract base class with decision methods returning Decision objects\n- **Key Methods**:\n  - `canAllocate(ShardRouting, RoutingNode, RoutingAllocation)` - allocation decision\n  - `canRemain(IndexMetadata, ShardRouting, RoutingNode, RoutingAllocation)` - residency decision\n  - `canRebalance(ShardRouting, RoutingAllocation)` - rebalancing permission\n  - `canForceAllocatePrimary(ShardRouting, RoutingNode, RoutingAllocation)` - force-allocate on lost node\n  - All methods default to `Decision.ALWAYS` if not overridden\n\n### 1.2 Existing Decider Examples\n\n#### **DiskThresholdDecider**\n- **Location**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/decider/DiskThresholdDecider.java`\n- **Purpose**: Prevents allocation to disk-full nodes\n- **Settings**:\n  - `cluster.routing.allocation.disk.watermark.low` - new allocations blocked above this\n  - `cluster.routing.allocation.disk.watermark.high` - shards must relocate above this\n  - `index.routing.allocation.disk.watermark.ignore` - per-index override\n\n#### **AwarenessAllocationDecider**\n- **Location**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/decider/AwarenessAllocationDecider.java`\n- **Purpose**: Distributes replicas across rack/zone awareness attributes\n- **Settings**:\n  - `cluster.routing.allocation.awareness.attributes` - which attributes to honor\n  - `cluster.routing.allocation.awareness.force.{attribute}.values` - forced group sizes\n\n---\n\n## 2. Problem Statement & Goals\n\n### 2.1 Current Limitation\n\nToday, Elasticsearch allocates shards uniformly across all data nodes based on balance metrics (shard count, disk usage, write load). It does **not** consider:\n- Node performance characteristics (CPU, memory speed, disk type)\n- Index criticality or SLA requirements\n- Tiered node infrastructure (hot/warm/cold are tier-based, not performance-based)\n\n### 2.2 Desired Capability\n\n**Priority-aware allocation** allows operators to:\n1. Mark critical indices with a `priority` level (e.g., 1-100)\n2. Tag nodes with performance tiers (e.g., `node_tier: premium`, `node_tier: standard`)\n3. Have the allocator **prefer** placing high-priority shards on high-tier nodes\n4. Fall back to standard nodes if insufficient premium capacity exists\n\n### 2.3 Design Goals\n\n1. **Non-intrusive**: Integrate with existing allocator without major refactoring\n2. **Composable**: Work alongside existing deciders (DiskThreshold, Awareness, etc.)\n3. **Configurable**: Allow operators to tune priority behavior per-cluster\n4. **Observable**: Clear logging/explain API output for why shards were/weren't allocated\n5. **Safe**: Graceful degradation\u2014critical shards still allocate even to lower-tier nodes\n\n---\n\n## 3. Proposed Design: PriorityShardsAllocator\n\n### 3.1 Architecture\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 AllocationService (cluster-wide routing orchestration)          \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                              \u2502\n                              \u25bc\n                    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n                    \u2502 ShardsAllocator      \u2502\n                    \u2502 (pluggable)          \u2502\n                    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                              \u2502\n              \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n              \u25bc               \u25bc               \u25bc\n    BalancedShardsAllocator   \u2502    PriorityShardsAllocator\n                         (new)\u2502    (new - wrapper/extension)\n                              \u2502\n              \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2534\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n              \u2502   AllocationDeciders chain    \u2502\n              \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                    \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u2502\n    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n    \u25bc               \u25bc  \u25bc  \u25bc  \u25bc  \u25bc  \u25bc  \u25bc               \u25bc\n Disk           Enable Awareness Same... Filter  PriorityAllocationDecider\n Threshold      Alloc  Decider   Shard           (new)\n Decider\n```\n\n### 3.2 Core Components\n\n#### **Component 1: Index Setting for Priority**\n\n**Name**: `index.routing.allocation.priority`\n**Type**: Integer\n**Default**: 50\n**Range**: 0-100\n**Scope**: Index\n**Dynamic**: Yes\n\n**Definition** (in `IndexMetadata.java`):\n```java\npublic static final String SETTING_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY = \"index.routing.allocation.priority\";\npublic static final Setting<Integer> INDEX_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_SETTING = Setting.intSetting(\n    \"index.routing.allocation.priority\",\n    50,  // default: medium priority\n    0,   // minimum\n    100, // maximum\n    Property.Dynamic,\n    Property.IndexScope\n);\n```\n\n**Usage Example**:\n```bash\nPUT /critical-app/_settings\n{\n  \"index.routing.allocation.priority\": 100  # highest priority\n}\n\nPUT /cache-index/_settings\n{\n  \"index.routing.allocation.priority\": 10   # lowest priority\n}\n```\n\n#### **Component 2: Node Attribute for Tier Classification**\n\n**Name**: `node.attr.allocation_tier` (operator-configured)\n**Example Values**: `premium`, `standard`, `basic`, `cold`\n\n**Configuration** (in elasticsearch.yml):\n```yaml\n# Premium nodes (fast SSD, 256GB RAM, 16 cores)\nnode.name: premium-node-1\nnode.attr.allocation_tier: premium\n\n# Standard nodes (regular SSD, 64GB RAM, 8 cores)\nnode.name: standard-node-1\nnode.attr.allocation_tier: standard\n```\n\n#### **Component 3: PriorityAllocationDecider**\n\n**Location**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/decider/PriorityAllocationDecider.java`\n\n**Responsibilities**:\n1. Extract priority from IndexMetadata\n2. Classify node as `premium` or `standard` (configurable)\n3. Implement soft constraints via scoring adjustments\n4. Implement hard constraints (e.g., reject allocating high-priority to low-tier nodes if alternatives exist)\n\n**Key Methods**:\n```java\npublic class PriorityAllocationDecider extends AllocationDecider {\n    public static final Setting<Boolean> CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_ENABLED =\n        Setting.boolSetting(\n            \"cluster.routing.allocation.priority.enabled\",\n            true,\n            Property.Dynamic,\n            Property.NodeScope\n        );\n\n    public static final Setting<List<String>> CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PREMIUM_TIERS =\n        Setting.stringListSetting(\n            \"cluster.routing.allocation.priority.premium_tiers\",\n            List.of(\"premium\"),\n            Property.Dynamic,\n            Property.NodeScope\n        );\n\n    @Override\n    public Decision canAllocate(ShardRouting shardRouting, RoutingNode node, RoutingAllocation allocation) {\n        // If feature disabled, always allow\n        if (!enabled) return Decision.ALWAYS;\n\n        // Get shard's index priority\n        IndexMetadata indexMetadata = allocation.metadata().getIndexSafe(shardRouting.index());\n        int indexPriority = getIndexPriority(indexMetadata);\n\n        // Get node's tier classification\n        String nodeTier = getNodeTier(node);\n\n        // Decision logic:\n        // 1. If index priority >= threshold AND node is premium tier: YES\n        // 2. If index priority >= threshold AND node is standard: THROTTLE (soft constraint)\n        // 3. If index priority < threshold: YES (standard allocation)\n\n        return decideAllocation(indexPriority, nodeTier);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### **Component 4: PriorityShardsAllocator (Optional Extension)**\n\n**Purpose**: A wrapper allocator that prioritizes shards by priority level\n**Location**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/allocator/PriorityShardsAllocator.java`\n\n**Design**:\n- Wraps or extends BalancedShardsAllocator\n- Reorders shard assignment queue by priority (highest-priority shards assigned first)\n- Delegates actual balancing to BalancedShardsAllocator\n- Ensures high-priority shards get \"first pick\" of available slots\n\n```java\npublic class PriorityShardsAllocator implements ShardsAllocator {\n    private final BalancedShardsAllocator delegate;\n\n    @Override\n    public void allocate(RoutingAllocation allocation) {\n        // Sort unassigned shards by priority (descending)\n        sortUnassignedShardsByPriority(allocation);\n\n        // Delegate to BalancedShardsAllocator for actual allocation\n        delegate.allocate(allocation);\n    }\n\n    private void sortUnassignedShardsByPriority(RoutingAllocation allocation) {\n        // Extract index priorities and reorder routing nodes' shard queues\n        RoutingNodes routingNodes = allocation.routingNodes();\n        routingNodes.unassigned().sort((shard1, shard2) -> {\n            int priority1 = getIndexPriority(allocation, shard1);\n            int priority2 = getIndexPriority(allocation, shard2);\n            return Integer.compare(priority2, priority1); // descending\n        });\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Integration with Existing Components\n\n### 4.1 AllocationDeciders Composition\n\n**Where PriorityAllocationDecider Fits**:\n\nThe PriorityAllocationDecider is registered in the decider chain (in AllocationService or RoutingAllocation initialization):\n\n```\nAllocationDeciders chain:\n1. EnableAllocationDecider        (check index.routing.allocation.enable)\n2. RebalanceOnlyWhenActiveDecider (wait for primaries to become active)\n3. DiskThresholdDecider           (check free disk space)\n4. AwarenessAllocationDecider     (check rack/zone awareness)\n5. FilterAllocationDecider        (check include/exclude/require filters)\n6. PriorityAllocationDecider      (NEW - apply priority preferences)\n7. SameShardAllocationDecider     (prevent primary/replica on same node)\n... other deciders ...\n```\n\n**Decision Logic**:\n- Each decider in sequence is queried via `canAllocate(shard, node, allocation)`\n- Chain uses **fail-fast AND semantics**: first NO result blocks the allocation\n- PriorityAllocationDecider returns THROTTLE for soft constraints (prefer premium nodes)\n- PriorityAllocationDecider returns YES/NO based on hard constraints (must allocate somewhere)\n\n### 4.2 Interaction with DiskThresholdDecider\n\n**Scenario**: High-priority index needs to allocate, but only disk-full nodes available\n\n**Behavior**:\n1. PriorityAllocationDecider allows allocation (priority >= some threshold)\n2. DiskThresholdDecider may still block (disk above watermark)\n3. **Result**: Shard stays unassigned or uses force-allocate path\n4. **Policy**: Disk constraints take precedence over priority preferences (safety first)\n\n### 4.3 Interaction with AwarenessAllocationDecider\n\n**Scenario**: High-priority index with awareness requirement (e.g., replicas on different racks)\n\n**Behavior**:\n1. AwarenessAllocationDecider enforces rack/zone distribution first\n2. Within rack constraints, PriorityAllocationDecider prefers premium nodes\n3. **Example**:\n   - Rack A: 1 premium node (100MB free), 2 standard nodes (1GB free each)\n   - High-priority shard for Rack A chooses premium node\n   - (assumes disk space sufficient in all)\n\n---\n\n## 5. API Changes & Additions\n\n### 5.1 Index Settings\n\n**New Setting**: `index.routing.allocation.priority`\n- Type: Integer (0-100)\n- Default: 50\n- Scope: Index\n- Dynamic: Yes\n- API: `PUT /index/_settings { \"index.routing.allocation.priority\": 75 }`\n\n### 5.2 Cluster Settings\n\n**New Settings**:\n\n| Setting | Type | Default | Purpose |\n|---------|------|---------|---------|\n| `cluster.routing.allocation.priority.enabled` | Boolean | true | Enable/disable feature |\n| `cluster.routing.allocation.priority.premium_tiers` | List[String] | [\"premium\"] | Node tier names considered premium |\n| `cluster.routing.allocation.priority.threshold` | Integer | 70 | Priority value above which prefer premium nodes |\n\n### 5.3 Cluster Explain API Enhancement\n\n**Extended Output** (from existing `GET /_cluster/allocation/explain`):\n\n```json\n{\n  \"shard\": {\n    \"index\": \"critical-app\",\n    \"index_priority\": 100,\n    \"id\": 0,\n    \"primary\": true\n  },\n  \"assigned\": false,\n  \"allocation_delay\": \"0ms\",\n  \"remaining_delay\": \"...\",\n  \"decisions\": [\n    {\n      \"decider\": \"enable\",\n      \"decision\": \"YES\",\n      \"explanation\": \"all allocation decisions are enabled\"\n    },\n    {\n      \"decider\": \"priority_allocation\",\n      \"decision\": \"THROTTLE\",\n      \"explanation\": \"shard has high priority (100); prefer premium tier nodes, but none available; will allocate to standard node\"\n    },\n    {\n      \"decider\": \"disk_threshold\",\n      \"decision\": \"YES\",\n      \"explanation\": \"enough disk space available\"\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Implementation Roadmap\n\n### Phase 1: Foundation\n- Add `INDEX_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_SETTING` to IndexMetadata\n- Create `PriorityAllocationDecider` with basic logic\n- Register decider in AllocationService\n\n### Phase 2: Allocator Extension\n- Create `PriorityShardsAllocator` wrapper\n- Implement shard queue reordering\n- Add configuration settings for tiers\n\n### Phase 3: Integration & Testing\n- Update Explain API to show priority decisions\n- Add cluster/index-level settings\n- Comprehensive test suite (unit + integration)\n\n### Phase 4: Documentation & Observability\n- Operator documentation (how to enable, configure)\n- Troubleshooting guides\n- Metrics for priority allocation success rates\n\n---\n\n## 7. Behavior Examples\n\n### Example 1: Simple Priority Allocation\n\n**Cluster Setup**:\n- Node-1: `allocation_tier=premium`, 500GB disk\n- Node-2: `allocation_tier=standard`, 500GB disk\n\n**Index Setup**:\n- `critical-index`: priority=100\n- `cache-index`: priority=10\n\n**Allocation Behavior**:\n1. `critical-index` shards allocate first and prefer Node-1 (premium)\n2. `cache-index` shards allocate to remaining space, can use Node-2 (standard)\n3. If Node-1 fills up, `critical-index` shards still allocate to Node-2\n\n### Example 2: Awareness + Priority\n\n**Cluster Setup**:\n- Rack A: premium-node-1, standard-node-2\n- Rack B: premium-node-3, standard-node-4\n\n**Replication Constraint**: Replicas must be on different racks\n**High-Priority Shard**: priority=90\n\n**Allocation**:\n1. Primary \u2192 Rack A's premium-node-1\n2. Replica \u2192 Rack B's premium-node-3 (respects awareness + preference)\n\n### Example 3: Degradation Under Load\n\n**Cluster Setup**:\n- 2 premium nodes (90% full)\n- 3 standard nodes (10% full)\n\n**Incoming Shard**: priority=100\n\n**Behavior**:\n1. Try premium nodes first (via THROTTLE decision)\n2. Premium nodes full, allocation blocked\n3. Fall back to standard nodes (via force-allocate or next phase)\n4. Shard allocates to standard node (graceful degradation)\n\n---\n\n## 8. Backward Compatibility\n\n### 8.1 Default Behavior\n\n- Feature disabled by default (opt-in via settings)\n- All indices default to priority=50 (middle of range)\n- Nodes without `allocation_tier` attribute treated as standard tier\n- Existing allocation logic unchanged if feature is disabled\n\n### 8.2 Upgrade Path\n\n1. Deploy new Elasticsearch version\n2. Feature defaults to enabled but with neutral priority thresholds\n3. No change to existing cluster behavior\n4. Operators gradually enable priority constraints\n\n---\n\n## 9. Observability & Debugging\n\n### 9.1 Logging\n\nPriorityAllocationDecider logs at TRACE level:\n```\n[priority_allocation] shard [index/1], priority=90, trying node [node-1], tier=premium -> allowed\n[priority_allocation] shard [index/1], priority=90, trying node [node-2], tier=standard -> throttled (prefer premium)\n```\n\n### 9.2 Explain API\n\nExample query:\n```bash\nGET /_cluster/allocation/explain\n{\n  \"index\": \"critical-app\",\n  \"shard\": 0,\n  \"primary\": true\n}\n```\n\n### 9.3 Metrics\n\n(Future enhancement):\n- `elasticsearch.routing.allocation.priority.high_tier_allocations` - count of high-priority shards on premium nodes\n- `elasticsearch.routing.allocation.priority.degraded_allocations` - count of high-priority shards on standard nodes\n\n---\n\n## 10. Security Considerations\n\n1. **Index Priority as User Input**: Index priority is settable by any user with index permissions\n   - **Mitigation**: Operators can cap priority via role-based settings restrictions\n\n2. **Resource Starvation**: Low-priority indices might starve for premium node resources\n   - **Mitigation**: Set reasonable defaults; operators can adjust thresholds\n\n3. **Audit Trail**: Track priority-based allocation decisions for compliance\n   - **Mitigation**: Enhanced logging + explain API output\n\n---\n\n## 11. Performance Considerations\n\n1. **Shard Queue Sorting** (in PriorityShardsAllocator):\n   - O(n log n) operation once per allocation round\n   - n = number of unassigned shards (typically < 1000 in most clusters)\n   - Negligible impact\n\n2. **Decider Invocation** (in PriorityAllocationDecider):\n   - O(1) per shard-node pair (simple priority lookup + tier check)\n   - No additional cluster state lookups\n\n3. **Overall Impact**: Negligible; allocation is already O(n\u00b2) in worst case\n\n---\n\n## 12. Testing Strategy\n\n### Unit Tests\n- PriorityAllocationDecider decision logic\n- Priority extraction from IndexMetadata\n- Node tier classification\n\n### Integration Tests\n- Multi-node cluster allocation scenarios\n- Mixed priority indices\n- Awareness + priority interactions\n- Disk threshold + priority interactions\n\n### Chaos Tests\n- Node failures with high/low-priority indices\n- Dynamic priority/tier changes\n- Large unassigned shard queues\n\n---\n\n## 13. References\n\n### Existing Components\n- **ShardsAllocator**: `server/src/main/java/.../allocation/allocator/ShardsAllocator.java`\n- **BalancedShardsAllocator**: `server/src/main/java/.../allocation/allocator/BalancedShardsAllocator.java`\n- **AllocationDecider**: `server/src/main/java/.../allocation/decider/AllocationDecider.java`\n- **AllocationDeciders**: `server/src/main/java/.../allocation/decider/AllocationDeciders.java`\n- **DiskThresholdDecider**: `server/src/main/java/.../allocation/decider/DiskThresholdDecider.java`\n- **AwarenessAllocationDecider**: `server/src/main/java/.../allocation/decider/AwarenessAllocationDecider.java`\n\n### Configuration\n- **IndexMetadata**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/metadata/IndexMetadata.java` (settings definitions)\n- **ClusterSettings**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/common/settings/ClusterSettings.java` (cluster-wide settings)\n\n### Testing\n- **DesiredBalanceComputerTests**: `server/src/test/java/.../allocation/allocator/DesiredBalanceComputerTests.java`\n- **AwarenessAllocationDeciderTests**: (search tests directory)\n\n---\n\n## 14. Success Criteria\n\n\u2705 **Design Review Completion**:\n- [x] Architecture clearly defined with component interactions\n- [x] Integration points identified with existing deciders\n- [x] API/settings specified\n- [x] Backward compatibility ensured\n- [x] Example scenarios provided\n\n\u2705 **Skeleton Code Completion**:\n- [x] PriorityShardsAllocator class structure (file generated)\n- [x] PriorityAllocationDecider framework (file generated)\n- [x] Setting definitions (in-code examples)\n- [x] Integration hooks documented\n\n**Next Steps (Implementation Phase)**:\n- Implement PriorityAllocationDecider decision logic\n- Implement PriorityShardsAllocator delegation\n- Add configuration settings to AllocationService\n- Write comprehensive test suite\n- Integration testing with real cluster scenarios\n",

  "content": "# Priority-Based Shard Allocation Strategy Design\n\n## Executive Summary\n\nThis document describes the design of a new `PriorityShardsAllocator` component for Elasticsearch that extends the existing shard allocation framework to support **priority-aware allocation**. The allocator enables critical indices to be preferentially placed on faster (higher-capacity or better-performing) nodes within the cluster.\n\n---\n\n## 1. Current Architecture Overview\n\n### 1.1 Existing Allocation Framework\n\nElasticsearch's shard allocation is based on a **pluggable architecture** with three core components:\n\n#### **ShardsAllocator Interface**\n- **Location**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/allocator/ShardsAllocator.java`\n- **Responsibilities**:\n  - `allocate(RoutingAllocation)` - Main allocation method\n  - `allocate(RoutingAllocation, ActionListener<Void>)` - Async variant\n  - `decideShardAllocation(ShardRouting, RoutingAllocation)` - Explain API support\n  - `execute(RoutingAllocation, AllocationCommands, ...)` - Execute explicit commands\n\n#### **BalancedShardsAllocator**\n- **Location**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/allocator/BalancedShardsAllocator.java`\n- **Current Implementation**: Balances shards using weighted function approach\n- **Balance Factors**:\n  - Shard count balance (cluster.routing.allocation.balance.shard)\n  - Index spread balance (cluster.routing.allocation.balance.index)\n  - Write load balance (cluster.routing.allocation.balance.write_load)\n  - Disk usage balance (cluster.routing.allocation.balance.disk_usage)\n- **Design Pattern**: Uses WeightFunction to compute node scores; allocates to node with highest score\n\n#### **AllocationDeciders Composition**\n- **Location**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/decider/AllocationDeciders.java`\n- **Purpose**: Combines multiple AllocationDecider instances using **fail-fast AND logic**\n  - Returns YES (proceed), THROTTLE (rate-limit), or NO (reject)\n  - First NO result blocks allocation\n- **Methods**:\n  - `canAllocate(ShardRouting, RoutingNode, RoutingAllocation)`\n  - `canRebalance(ShardRouting, RoutingAllocation)`\n  - `canRemain(ShardRouting, RoutingNode, RoutingAllocation)`\n  - `shouldAutoExpandToNode(IndexMetadata, DiscoveryNode, RoutingAllocation)`\n\n#### **AllocationDecider Base Class**\n- **Location**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/decider/AllocationDecider.java`\n- **Design**: Abstract base class with decision methods returning Decision objects\n- **Key Methods**:\n  - `canAllocate(ShardRouting, RoutingNode, RoutingAllocation)` - allocation decision\n  - `canRemain(IndexMetadata, ShardRouting, RoutingNode, RoutingAllocation)` - residency decision\n  - `canRebalance(ShardRouting, RoutingAllocation)` - rebalancing permission\n  - `canForceAllocatePrimary(ShardRouting, RoutingNode, RoutingAllocation)` - force-allocate on lost node\n  - All methods default to `Decision.ALWAYS` if not overridden\n\n### 1.2 Existing Decider Examples\n\n#### **DiskThresholdDecider**\n- **Location**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/decider/DiskThresholdDecider.java`\n- **Purpose**: Prevents allocation to disk-full nodes\n- **Settings**:\n  - `cluster.routing.allocation.disk.watermark.low` - new allocations blocked above this\n  - `cluster.routing.allocation.disk.watermark.high` - shards must relocate above this\n  - `index.routing.allocation.disk.watermark.ignore` - per-index override\n\n#### **AwarenessAllocationDecider**\n- **Location**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/decider/AwarenessAllocationDecider.java`\n- **Purpose**: Distributes replicas across rack/zone awareness attributes\n- **Settings**:\n  - `cluster.routing.allocation.awareness.attributes` - which attributes to honor\n  - `cluster.routing.allocation.awareness.force.{attribute}.values` - forced group sizes\n\n---\n\n## 2. Problem Statement & Goals\n\n### 2.1 Current Limitation\n\nToday, Elasticsearch allocates shards uniformly across all data nodes based on balance metrics (shard count, disk usage, write load). It does **not** consider:\n- Node performance characteristics (CPU, memory speed, disk type)\n- Index criticality or SLA requirements\n- Tiered node infrastructure (hot/warm/cold are tier-based, not performance-based)\n\n### 2.2 Desired Capability\n\n**Priority-aware allocation** allows operators to:\n1. Mark critical indices with a `priority` level (e.g., 1-100)\n2. Tag nodes with performance tiers (e.g., `node_tier: premium`, `node_tier: standard`)\n3. Have the allocator **prefer** placing high-priority shards on high-tier nodes\n4. Fall back to standard nodes if insufficient premium capacity exists\n\n### 2.3 Design Goals\n\n1. **Non-intrusive**: Integrate with existing allocator without major refactoring\n2. **Composable**: Work alongside existing deciders (DiskThreshold, Awareness, etc.)\n3. **Configurable**: Allow operators to tune priority behavior per-cluster\n4. **Observable**: Clear logging/explain API output for why shards were/weren't allocated\n5. **Safe**: Graceful degradation\u2014critical shards still allocate even to lower-tier nodes\n\n---\n\n## 3. Proposed Design: PriorityShardsAllocator\n\n### 3.1 Architecture\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 AllocationService (cluster-wide routing orchestration)          \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                              \u2502\n                              \u25bc\n                    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n                    \u2502 ShardsAllocator      \u2502\n                    \u2502 (pluggable)          \u2502\n                    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                              \u2502\n              \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n              \u25bc               \u25bc               \u25bc\n    BalancedShardsAllocator   \u2502    PriorityShardsAllocator\n                         (new)\u2502    (new - wrapper/extension)\n                              \u2502\n              \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2534\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n              \u2502   AllocationDeciders chain    \u2502\n              \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                    \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u2502\n    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n    \u25bc               \u25bc  \u25bc  \u25bc  \u25bc  \u25bc  \u25bc  \u25bc               \u25bc\n Disk           Enable Awareness Same... Filter  PriorityAllocationDecider\n Threshold      Alloc  Decider   Shard           (new)\n Decider\n```\n\n### 3.2 Core Components\n\n#### **Component 1: Index Setting for Priority**\n\n**Name**: `index.routing.allocation.priority`\n**Type**: Integer\n**Default**: 50\n**Range**: 0-100\n**Scope**: Index\n**Dynamic**: Yes\n\n**Definition** (in `IndexMetadata.java`):\n```java\npublic static final String SETTING_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY = \"index.routing.allocation.priority\";\npublic static final Setting<Integer> INDEX_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_SETTING = Setting.intSetting(\n    \"index.routing.allocation.priority\",\n    50,  // default: medium priority\n    0,   // minimum\n    100, // maximum\n    Property.Dynamic,\n    Property.IndexScope\n);\n```\n\n**Usage Example**:\n```bash\nPUT /critical-app/_settings\n{\n  \"index.routing.allocation.priority\": 100  # highest priority\n}\n\nPUT /cache-index/_settings\n{\n  \"index.routing.allocation.priority\": 10   # lowest priority\n}\n```\n\n#### **Component 2: Node Attribute for Tier Classification**\n\n**Name**: `node.attr.allocation_tier` (operator-configured)\n**Example Values**: `premium`, `standard`, `basic`, `cold`\n\n**Configuration** (in elasticsearch.yml):\n```yaml\n# Premium nodes (fast SSD, 256GB RAM, 16 cores)\nnode.name: premium-node-1\nnode.attr.allocation_tier: premium\n\n# Standard nodes (regular SSD, 64GB RAM, 8 cores)\nnode.name: standard-node-1\nnode.attr.allocation_tier: standard\n```\n\n#### **Component 3: PriorityAllocationDecider**\n\n**Location**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/decider/PriorityAllocationDecider.java`\n\n**Responsibilities**:\n1. Extract priority from IndexMetadata\n2. Classify node as `premium` or `standard` (configurable)\n3. Implement soft constraints via scoring adjustments\n4. Implement hard constraints (e.g., reject allocating high-priority to low-tier nodes if alternatives exist)\n\n**Key Methods**:\n```java\npublic class PriorityAllocationDecider extends AllocationDecider {\n    public static final Setting<Boolean> CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_ENABLED =\n        Setting.boolSetting(\n            \"cluster.routing.allocation.priority.enabled\",\n            true,\n            Property.Dynamic,\n            Property.NodeScope\n        );\n\n    public static final Setting<List<String>> CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PREMIUM_TIERS =\n        Setting.stringListSetting(\n            \"cluster.routing.allocation.priority.premium_tiers\",\n            List.of(\"premium\"),\n            Property.Dynamic,\n            Property.NodeScope\n        );\n\n    @Override\n    public Decision canAllocate(ShardRouting shardRouting, RoutingNode node, RoutingAllocation allocation) {\n        // If feature disabled, always allow\n        if (!enabled) return Decision.ALWAYS;\n\n        // Get shard's index priority\n        IndexMetadata indexMetadata = allocation.metadata().getIndexSafe(shardRouting.index());\n        int indexPriority = getIndexPriority(indexMetadata);\n\n        // Get node's tier classification\n        String nodeTier = getNodeTier(node);\n\n        // Decision logic:\n        // 1. If index priority >= threshold AND node is premium tier: YES\n        // 2. If index priority >= threshold AND node is standard: THROTTLE (soft constraint)\n        // 3. If index priority < threshold: YES (standard allocation)\n\n        return decideAllocation(indexPriority, nodeTier);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### **Component 4: PriorityShardsAllocator (Optional Extension)**\n\n**Purpose**: A wrapper allocator that prioritizes shards by priority level\n**Location**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/routing/allocation/allocator/PriorityShardsAllocator.java`\n\n**Design**:\n- Wraps or extends BalancedShardsAllocator\n- Reorders shard assignment queue by priority (highest-priority shards assigned first)\n- Delegates actual balancing to BalancedShardsAllocator\n- Ensures high-priority shards get \"first pick\" of available slots\n\n```java\npublic class PriorityShardsAllocator implements ShardsAllocator {\n    private final BalancedShardsAllocator delegate;\n\n    @Override\n    public void allocate(RoutingAllocation allocation) {\n        // Sort unassigned shards by priority (descending)\n        sortUnassignedShardsByPriority(allocation);\n\n        // Delegate to BalancedShardsAllocator for actual allocation\n        delegate.allocate(allocation);\n    }\n\n    private void sortUnassignedShardsByPriority(RoutingAllocation allocation) {\n        // Extract index priorities and reorder routing nodes' shard queues\n        RoutingNodes routingNodes = allocation.routingNodes();\n        routingNodes.unassigned().sort((shard1, shard2) -> {\n            int priority1 = getIndexPriority(allocation, shard1);\n            int priority2 = getIndexPriority(allocation, shard2);\n            return Integer.compare(priority2, priority1); // descending\n        });\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Integration with Existing Components\n\n### 4.1 AllocationDeciders Composition\n\n**Where PriorityAllocationDecider Fits**:\n\nThe PriorityAllocationDecider is registered in the decider chain (in AllocationService or RoutingAllocation initialization):\n\n```\nAllocationDeciders chain:\n1. EnableAllocationDecider        (check index.routing.allocation.enable)\n2. RebalanceOnlyWhenActiveDecider (wait for primaries to become active)\n3. DiskThresholdDecider           (check free disk space)\n4. AwarenessAllocationDecider     (check rack/zone awareness)\n5. FilterAllocationDecider        (check include/exclude/require filters)\n6. PriorityAllocationDecider      (NEW - apply priority preferences)\n7. SameShardAllocationDecider     (prevent primary/replica on same node)\n... other deciders ...\n```\n\n**Decision Logic**:\n- Each decider in sequence is queried via `canAllocate(shard, node, allocation)`\n- Chain uses **fail-fast AND semantics**: first NO result blocks the allocation\n- PriorityAllocationDecider returns THROTTLE for soft constraints (prefer premium nodes)\n- PriorityAllocationDecider returns YES/NO based on hard constraints (must allocate somewhere)\n\n### 4.2 Interaction with DiskThresholdDecider\n\n**Scenario**: High-priority index needs to allocate, but only disk-full nodes available\n\n**Behavior**:\n1. PriorityAllocationDecider allows allocation (priority >= some threshold)\n2. DiskThresholdDecider may still block (disk above watermark)\n3. **Result**: Shard stays unassigned or uses force-allocate path\n4. **Policy**: Disk constraints take precedence over priority preferences (safety first)\n\n### 4.3 Interaction with AwarenessAllocationDecider\n\n**Scenario**: High-priority index with awareness requirement (e.g., replicas on different racks)\n\n**Behavior**:\n1. AwarenessAllocationDecider enforces rack/zone distribution first\n2. Within rack constraints, PriorityAllocationDecider prefers premium nodes\n3. **Example**:\n   - Rack A: 1 premium node (100MB free), 2 standard nodes (1GB free each)\n   - High-priority shard for Rack A chooses premium node\n   - (assumes disk space sufficient in all)\n\n---\n\n## 5. API Changes & Additions\n\n### 5.1 Index Settings\n\n**New Setting**: `index.routing.allocation.priority`\n- Type: Integer (0-100)\n- Default: 50\n- Scope: Index\n- Dynamic: Yes\n- API: `PUT /index/_settings { \"index.routing.allocation.priority\": 75 }`\n\n### 5.2 Cluster Settings\n\n**New Settings**:\n\n| Setting | Type | Default | Purpose |\n|---------|------|---------|---------|\n| `cluster.routing.allocation.priority.enabled` | Boolean | true | Enable/disable feature |\n| `cluster.routing.allocation.priority.premium_tiers` | List[String] | [\"premium\"] | Node tier names considered premium |\n| `cluster.routing.allocation.priority.threshold` | Integer | 70 | Priority value above which prefer premium nodes |\n\n### 5.3 Cluster Explain API Enhancement\n\n**Extended Output** (from existing `GET /_cluster/allocation/explain`):\n\n```json\n{\n  \"shard\": {\n    \"index\": \"critical-app\",\n    \"index_priority\": 100,\n    \"id\": 0,\n    \"primary\": true\n  },\n  \"assigned\": false,\n  \"allocation_delay\": \"0ms\",\n  \"remaining_delay\": \"...\",\n  \"decisions\": [\n    {\n      \"decider\": \"enable\",\n      \"decision\": \"YES\",\n      \"explanation\": \"all allocation decisions are enabled\"\n    },\n    {\n      \"decider\": \"priority_allocation\",\n      \"decision\": \"THROTTLE\",\n      \"explanation\": \"shard has high priority (100); prefer premium tier nodes, but none available; will allocate to standard node\"\n    },\n    {\n      \"decider\": \"disk_threshold\",\n      \"decision\": \"YES\",\n      \"explanation\": \"enough disk space available\"\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Implementation Roadmap\n\n### Phase 1: Foundation\n- Add `INDEX_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_SETTING` to IndexMetadata\n- Create `PriorityAllocationDecider` with basic logic\n- Register decider in AllocationService\n\n### Phase 2: Allocator Extension\n- Create `PriorityShardsAllocator` wrapper\n- Implement shard queue reordering\n- Add configuration settings for tiers\n\n### Phase 3: Integration & Testing\n- Update Explain API to show priority decisions\n- Add cluster/index-level settings\n- Comprehensive test suite (unit + integration)\n\n### Phase 4: Documentation & Observability\n- Operator documentation (how to enable, configure)\n- Troubleshooting guides\n- Metrics for priority allocation success rates\n\n---\n\n## 7. Behavior Examples\n\n### Example 1: Simple Priority Allocation\n\n**Cluster Setup**:\n- Node-1: `allocation_tier=premium`, 500GB disk\n- Node-2: `allocation_tier=standard`, 500GB disk\n\n**Index Setup**:\n- `critical-index`: priority=100\n- `cache-index`: priority=10\n\n**Allocation Behavior**:\n1. `critical-index` shards allocate first and prefer Node-1 (premium)\n2. `cache-index` shards allocate to remaining space, can use Node-2 (standard)\n3. If Node-1 fills up, `critical-index` shards still allocate to Node-2\n\n### Example 2: Awareness + Priority\n\n**Cluster Setup**:\n- Rack A: premium-node-1, standard-node-2\n- Rack B: premium-node-3, standard-node-4\n\n**Replication Constraint**: Replicas must be on different racks\n**High-Priority Shard**: priority=90\n\n**Allocation**:\n1. Primary \u2192 Rack A's premium-node-1\n2. Replica \u2192 Rack B's premium-node-3 (respects awareness + preference)\n\n### Example 3: Degradation Under Load\n\n**Cluster Setup**:\n- 2 premium nodes (90% full)\n- 3 standard nodes (10% full)\n\n**Incoming Shard**: priority=100\n\n**Behavior**:\n1. Try premium nodes first (via THROTTLE decision)\n2. Premium nodes full, allocation blocked\n3. Fall back to standard nodes (via force-allocate or next phase)\n4. Shard allocates to standard node (graceful degradation)\n\n---\n\n## 8. Backward Compatibility\n\n### 8.1 Default Behavior\n\n- Feature disabled by default (opt-in via settings)\n- All indices default to priority=50 (middle of range)\n- Nodes without `allocation_tier` attribute treated as standard tier\n- Existing allocation logic unchanged if feature is disabled\n\n### 8.2 Upgrade Path\n\n1. Deploy new Elasticsearch version\n2. Feature defaults to enabled but with neutral priority thresholds\n3. No change to existing cluster behavior\n4. Operators gradually enable priority constraints\n\n---\n\n## 9. Observability & Debugging\n\n### 9.1 Logging\n\nPriorityAllocationDecider logs at TRACE level:\n```\n[priority_allocation] shard [index/1], priority=90, trying node [node-1], tier=premium -> allowed\n[priority_allocation] shard [index/1], priority=90, trying node [node-2], tier=standard -> throttled (prefer premium)\n```\n\n### 9.2 Explain API\n\nExample query:\n```bash\nGET /_cluster/allocation/explain\n{\n  \"index\": \"critical-app\",\n  \"shard\": 0,\n  \"primary\": true\n}\n```\n\n### 9.3 Metrics\n\n(Future enhancement):\n- `elasticsearch.routing.allocation.priority.high_tier_allocations` - count of high-priority shards on premium nodes\n- `elasticsearch.routing.allocation.priority.degraded_allocations` - count of high-priority shards on standard nodes\n\n---\n\n## 10. Security Considerations\n\n1. **Index Priority as User Input**: Index priority is settable by any user with index permissions\n   - **Mitigation**: Operators can cap priority via role-based settings restrictions\n\n2. **Resource Starvation**: Low-priority indices might starve for premium node resources\n   - **Mitigation**: Set reasonable defaults; operators can adjust thresholds\n\n3. **Audit Trail**: Track priority-based allocation decisions for compliance\n   - **Mitigation**: Enhanced logging + explain API output\n\n---\n\n## 11. Performance Considerations\n\n1. **Shard Queue Sorting** (in PriorityShardsAllocator):\n   - O(n log n) operation once per allocation round\n   - n = number of unassigned shards (typically < 1000 in most clusters)\n   - Negligible impact\n\n2. **Decider Invocation** (in PriorityAllocationDecider):\n   - O(1) per shard-node pair (simple priority lookup + tier check)\n   - No additional cluster state lookups\n\n3. **Overall Impact**: Negligible; allocation is already O(n\u00b2) in worst case\n\n---\n\n## 12. Testing Strategy\n\n### Unit Tests\n- PriorityAllocationDecider decision logic\n- Priority extraction from IndexMetadata\n- Node tier classification\n\n### Integration Tests\n- Multi-node cluster allocation scenarios\n- Mixed priority indices\n- Awareness + priority interactions\n- Disk threshold + priority interactions\n\n### Chaos Tests\n- Node failures with high/low-priority indices\n- Dynamic priority/tier changes\n- Large unassigned shard queues\n\n---\n\n## 13. References\n\n### Existing Components\n- **ShardsAllocator**: `server/src/main/java/.../allocation/allocator/ShardsAllocator.java`\n- **BalancedShardsAllocator**: `server/src/main/java/.../allocation/allocator/BalancedShardsAllocator.java`\n- **AllocationDecider**: `server/src/main/java/.../allocation/decider/AllocationDecider.java`\n- **AllocationDeciders**: `server/src/main/java/.../allocation/decider/AllocationDeciders.java`\n- **DiskThresholdDecider**: `server/src/main/java/.../allocation/decider/DiskThresholdDecider.java`\n- **AwarenessAllocationDecider**: `server/src/main/java/.../allocation/decider/AwarenessAllocationDecider.java`\n\n### Configuration\n- **IndexMetadata**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/metadata/IndexMetadata.java` (settings definitions)\n- **ClusterSettings**: `server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/common/settings/ClusterSettings.java` (cluster-wide settings)\n\n### Testing\n- **DesiredBalanceComputerTests**: `server/src/test/java/.../allocation/allocator/DesiredBalanceComputerTests.java`\n- **AwarenessAllocationDeciderTests**: (search tests directory)\n\n---\n\n## 14. Success Criteria\n\n\u2705 **Design Review Completion**:\n- [x] Architecture clearly defined with component interactions\n- [x] Integration points identified with existing deciders\n- [x] API/settings specified\n- [x] Backward compatibility ensured\n- [x] Example scenarios provided\n\n\u2705 **Skeleton Code Completion**:\n- [x] PriorityShardsAllocator class structure (file generated)\n- [x] PriorityAllocationDecider framework (file generated)\n- [x] Setting definitions (in-code examples)\n- [x] Integration hooks documented\n\n**Next Steps (Implementation Phase)**:\n- Implement PriorityAllocationDecider decision logic\n- Implement PriorityShardsAllocator delegation\n- Add configuration settings to AllocationService\n- Write comprehensive test suite\n- Integration testing with real cluster scenarios\n",

  "content": "/*\n * Copyright Elasticsearch B.V. and/or licensed to Elasticsearch B.V. under one\n * or more contributor license agreements. Shards with higher priority\n * are processed first, ensuring critical indices receive \"first pick\" of available slots.\n * </p>\n *\n * <p>\n * This allocator works in conjunction with {@link PriorityAllocationDecider} to:\n * <ul>\n *   <li>Reorder the shard assignment queue by priority (highest-priority shards first)</li>\n *   <li>Delegate balancing decisions to the wrapped BalancedShardsAllocator</li>\n *   <li>Support soft constraints via THROTTLE decisions from PriorityAllocationDecider</li>\n * </ul>\n * </p>\n *\n * <h2>Configuration</h2>\n *\n * Enable or disable priority-aware allocation:\n * <pre>\n * cluster.routing.allocation.priority.enabled: true  (default)\n * </pre>\n *\n * Control which node tiers are considered premium:\n * <pre>\n * cluster.routing.allocation.priority.premium_tiers: [premium, hot]\n * </pre>\n *\n * Set the priority threshold above which to prefer premium nodes:\n * <pre>\n * cluster.routing.allocation.priority.threshold: 70\n * </pre>\n *\n * <h2>Index Settings</h2>\n *\n * Set index priority for shard allocation preferences:\n * <pre>\n * PUT /myindex/_settings\n * {\n *   \"index.routing.allocation.priority\": 100\n * }\n * </pre>\n *\n * @see PriorityAllocationDecider\n * @see BalancedShardsAllocator\n * @see IndexMetadata#INDEX_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_SETTING\n */\npublic class PriorityShardsAllocator implements ShardsAllocator {\n\n    private static final Logger logger = LogManager.getLogger(PriorityShardsAllocator.class);\n\n    /**\n     * Cluster-level setting to enable/disable priority-aware allocation.\n     * Defaults to true; set to false to revert to standard balanced allocation.\n     */\n    public static final Setting<Boolean> CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_ENABLED = Setting.boolSetting(\n        \"cluster.routing.allocation.priority.enabled\",\n        true,\n        Property.Dynamic,\n        Property.NodeScope\n    );\n\n    /**\n     * Cluster-level setting specifying which node tier names are considered premium.\n     * Shards with high priority prefer allocation to premium tier nodes.\n     * Example: [\"premium\", \"hot\"]\n     */\n    public static final Setting<List<String>> CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_PREMIUM_TIERS = Setting.stringListSetting(\n        \"cluster.routing.allocation.priority.premium_tiers\",\n        java.util.List.of(\"premium\"),\n        Property.Dynamic,\n        Property.NodeScope\n    );\n\n    /**\n     * Cluster-level setting specifying the priority threshold above which\n     * to apply premium tier preferences. Indices with priority >= threshold\n     * will prefer premium nodes, but can still allocate to standard nodes.\n     * Range: 0-100, Default: 70\n     */\n    public static final Setting<Integer> CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_THRESHOLD = Setting.intSetting(\n        \"cluster.routing.allocation.priority.threshold\",\n        70,\n        0,\n        100,\n        Property.Dynamic,\n        Property.NodeScope\n    );\n\n    /**\n     * Index-level setting specifying the priority of this index for shard allocation.\n     * Higher values indicate higher priority for placement on preferred (premium) nodes.\n     * Range: 0-100, Default: 50\n     */\n    public static final String INDEX_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY = \"index.routing.allocation.priority\";\n\n    // Volatile fields for dynamic configuration updates\n    private volatile boolean priorityAllocationEnabled;\n    private volatile List<String> premiumTiers;\n    private volatile int priorityThreshold;\n\n    // Delegate allocator for actual shard balancing\n    private final BalancedShardsAllocator delegateAllocator;\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a new PriorityShardsAllocator with default configuration.\n     * The delegate BalancedShardsAllocator uses standard settings.\n     */\n    public PriorityShardsAllocator() {\n        this.delegateAllocator = new BalancedShardsAllocator();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a new PriorityShardsAllocator with custom cluster settings.\n     * Registers dynamic setting listeners for priority configuration changes.\n     *\n     * @param clusterSettings the cluster settings to watch for priority configuration\n     * @param delegateAllocator the wrapped allocator for balancing decisions\n     */\n    @Inject\n    public PriorityShardsAllocator(\n        ClusterSettings clusterSettings,\n        BalancedShardsAllocator delegateAllocator\n    ) {\n        this.delegateAllocator = delegateAllocator;\n\n        // Initialize settings from cluster configuration\n        this.priorityAllocationEnabled = CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_ENABLED.get(clusterSettings.getSettings());\n        this.premiumTiers = CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_PREMIUM_TIERS.get(clusterSettings.getSettings());\n        this.priorityThreshold = CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_THRESHOLD.get(clusterSettings.getSettings());\n\n        // Register listeners for dynamic updates\n        clusterSettings.addSettingsUpdateConsumer(\n            CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_ENABLED,\n            this::setPriorityAllocationEnabled\n        );\n        clusterSettings.addSettingsUpdateConsumer(\n            CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_PREMIUM_TIERS,\n            this::setPremiumTiers\n        );\n        clusterSettings.addSettingsUpdateConsumer(\n            CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_THRESHOLD,\n            this::setPriorityThreshold\n        );\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Main allocation method. Sorts unassigned shards by priority and delegates\n     * to the wrapped BalancedShardsAllocator for actual allocation decisions.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * Algorithm:\n     * <ol>\n     *   <li>If priority allocation is disabled, delegate directly</li>\n     *   <li>Otherwise, sort unassigned shards by index priority (descending)</li>\n     *   <li>Invoke delegate allocator's allocate() method</li>\n     * </ol>\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param allocation the current routing allocation state\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void allocate(RoutingAllocation allocation) {\n        if (!priorityAllocationEnabled) {\n            // Feature disabled; use standard balanced allocation\n            delegateAllocator.allocate(allocation);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Sort unassigned shards by priority (highest first)\n        sortUnassignedShardsByPriority(allocation);\n\n        // Delegate to BalancedShardsAllocator for balanced shard distribution\n        delegateAllocator.allocate(allocation);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Async variant of allocate(). Delegates to the wrapped allocator's async method.\n     *\n     * @param allocation the current routing allocation state\n     * @param listener listener to be called once async allocation is complete\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void allocate(RoutingAllocation allocation, ActionListener<Void> listener) {\n        if (!priorityAllocationEnabled) {\n            delegateAllocator.allocate(allocation, listener);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        sortUnassignedShardsByPriority(allocation);\n        delegateAllocator.allocate(allocation, listener);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Executes explicit allocation commands. Delegates to the wrapped allocator.\n     *\n     * @param allocation the current routing allocation state\n     * @param commands the allocation commands to execute\n     * @param explain whether to return explain information\n     * @param retryFailed whether to reset the failed counter for retryable shards\n     * @return explanations for each executed command\n     */\n    @Override\n    public RoutingExplanations execute(\n        RoutingAllocation allocation,\n        AllocationCommands commands,\n        boolean explain,\n        boolean retryFailed\n    ) {\n        return delegateAllocator.execute(allocation, commands, explain, retryFailed);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns the allocation decision for a single shard. Queries the wrapped\n     * allocator for shard allocation decisions (used by the explain API).\n     *\n     * @param shard the shard routing to decide on\n     * @param allocation the current routing allocation state\n     * @return the allocation decision for this shard\n     */\n    @Override\n    public ShardAllocationDecision decideShardAllocation(ShardRouting shard, RoutingAllocation allocation) {\n        return delegateAllocator.decideShardAllocation(shard, allocation);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Sorts unassigned shards in the routing allocation by their index priority.\n     * Shards from indices with higher priority are moved to the front of the queue,\n     * ensuring they are considered first during allocation.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * The priority value is retrieved from {@link IndexMetadata} using\n     * the INDEX_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY setting. Indices without an explicit\n     * priority setting use the default value of 50.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * Time Complexity: O(n log n) where n = number of unassigned shards\n     * This is typically << 1000 shards in most clusters, making the overhead negligible.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param allocation the routing allocation containing the unassigned shards to sort\n     */\n    private void sortUnassignedShardsByPriority(RoutingAllocation allocation) {\n        try {\n            var unassignedShards = allocation.routingNodes().unassigned();\n            if (unassignedShards == null || unassignedShards.size() == 0) {\n                return; // No shards to sort\n            }\n\n            // Create a mutable list of shards sorted by priority (descending)\n            List<ShardRouting> shardsToSort = new ArrayList<>(unassignedShards.size());\n            for (ShardRouting shard : unassignedShards) {\n                shardsToSort.add(shard);\n            }\n\n            // Sort by index priority (descending: highest priority first)\n            shardsToSort.sort(\n                Comparator.comparingInt(\n                    (ShardRouting shard) -> getIndexPriority(allocation, shard)\n                ).reversed()\n            );\n\n            // Replace the unassigned shards iterator with sorted shards\n            // This requires calling internal routing nodes methods\n            // Note: This is pseudocode; actual implementation depends on\n            // RoutingNodes API for reordering\n            reorderUnassignedShards(allocation, shardsToSort);\n\n            if (logger.isDebugEnabled()) {\n                logger.debug(\n                    \"Sorted {} unassigned shards by priority (feature enabled)\",\n                    shardsToSort.size()\n                );\n            }\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            // Log error but don't fail allocation on sorting error\n            logger.warn(\"Failed to sort unassigned shards by priority; continuing with standard order\", e);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Reorders the unassigned shards in the routing nodes to match the priority-sorted list.\n     * This is a placeholder for the actual reordering implementation, which depends on\n     * the RoutingNodes API.\n     *\n     * @param allocation the routing allocation state\n     * @param sortedShards the shards sorted by priority (descending)\n     */\n    private void reorderUnassignedShards(RoutingAllocation allocation, List<ShardRouting> sortedShards) {\n        // TODO: Implement actual reordering using RoutingNodes API\n        // This may involve:\n        // 1. Clearing the current unassigned shards collection\n        // 2. Adding shards back in priority order\n        // OR\n        // 3. Using a custom iterator/wrapper that returns shards in priority order\n        //\n        // Example (pseudocode):\n        // RoutingNodes routingNodes = allocation.routingNodes();\n        // routingNodes.unassigned().clear();\n        // for (ShardRouting shard : sortedShards) {\n        //     routingNodes.unassigned().add(shard);\n        // }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Retrieves the priority value for an index from its metadata.\n     * Falls back to the default priority if not explicitly set.\n     *\n     * @param allocation the routing allocation state (contains cluster metadata)\n     * @param shard the shard whose index priority to retrieve\n     * @return the index priority (0-100), or default 50 if not set\n     */\n    private int getIndexPriority(RoutingAllocation allocation, ShardRouting shard) {\n        try {\n            IndexMetadata indexMetadata = allocation.metadata().getIndexSafe(shard.index());\n            // TODO: Extract priority from indexMetadata\n            // Pseudo-code:\n            // return indexMetadata.getSettings().getAsInt(\n            //     INDEX_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY,\n            //     50  // default priority\n            // );\n            return 50; // placeholder\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            logger.warn(\"Failed to retrieve priority for index [{}], using default\", shard.index(), e);\n            return 50; // default priority on error\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Determines if a node is classified as premium tier.\n     * Queries the node's attributes for a tier classification and checks\n     * if it matches one of the configured premium tiers.\n     *\n     * @param nodeName the name/ID of the node to check\n     * @param allocation the routing allocation state (contains node metadata)\n     * @return true if the node is classified as a premium tier node\n     */\n    private boolean isNodePremiumTier(String nodeName, RoutingAllocation allocation) {\n        try {\n            // TODO: Extract node attributes and check tier classification\n            // Pseudo-code:\n            // var node = allocation.nodes().get(nodeName);\n            // if (node == null) return false;\n            // String nodeTier = node.getAttributes().get(\"allocation_tier\");\n            // return premiumTiers.contains(nodeTier);\n            return false; // placeholder\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            logger.warn(\"Failed to determine tier for node [{}], assuming standard\", nodeName, e);\n            return false; // assume standard on error\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ============= Configuration Update Methods =============\n\n    /**\n     * Called when the priority allocation enabled setting is updated dynamically.\n     *\n     * @param enabled the new enabled state\n     */\n    private void setPriorityAllocationEnabled(boolean enabled) {\n        this.priorityAllocationEnabled = enabled;\n        logger.info(\"Priority-aware shard allocation is now {}\", enabled ? \"enabled\" : \"disabled\");\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Called when the premium tiers setting is updated dynamically.\n     *\n     * @param tiers the new list of premium tier names\n     */\n    private void setPremiumTiers(List<String> tiers) {\n        this.premiumTiers = threshold: {}\", threshold);\n    }\n\n    // ============= Getters for testing/debugging =============\n\n    /**\n     * Returns whether priority allocation is currently enabled.\n     *\n     * Returns the current priority threshold value.\n     *\n     * @return the priority threshold (0-100)\n     */\n    public int getPriorityThreshold() {\n        return priorityThreshold;\n    }\n}\n",

Shards with higher priority\n * are processed first, ensuring critical indices receive \"first pick\" of available slots.\n * </p>\n *\n * <p>\n * This allocator works in conjunction with {@link PriorityAllocationDecider} to:\n * <ul>\n *   <li>Reorder the shard assignment queue by priority (highest-priority shards first)</li>\n *   <li>Delegate balancing decisions to the wrapped BalancedShardsAllocator</li>\n *   <li>Support soft constraints via THROTTLE decisions from PriorityAllocationDecider</li>\n * </ul>\n * </p>\n *\n * <h2>Configuration</h2>\n *\n * Enable or disable priority-aware allocation:\n * <pre>\n * cluster.routing.allocation.priority.enabled: true  (default)\n * </pre>\n *\n * Control which node tiers are considered premium:\n * <pre>\n * cluster.routing.allocation.priority.premium_tiers: [premium, hot]\n * </pre>\n *\n * Set the priority threshold above which to prefer premium nodes:\n * <pre>\n * cluster.routing.allocation.priority.threshold: 70\n * </pre>\n *\n * <h2>Index Settings</h2>\n *\n * Set index priority for shard allocation preferences:\n * <pre>\n * PUT /myindex/_settings\n * {\n *   \"index.routing.allocation.priority\": 100\n * }\n * </pre>\n *\n * @see PriorityAllocationDecider\n * @see BalancedShardsAllocator\n * @see IndexMetadata#INDEX_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_SETTING\n */\npublic class PriorityShardsAllocator implements ShardsAllocator {\n\n    private static final Logger logger = LogManager.getLogger(PriorityShardsAllocator.class);\n\n    /**\n     * Cluster-level setting to enable/disable priority-aware allocation.\n     * Defaults to true; set to false to revert to standard balanced allocation.\n     */\n    public static final Setting<Boolean> CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_ENABLED = Setting.boolSetting(\n        \"cluster.routing.allocation.priority.enabled\",\n        true,\n        Property.Dynamic,\n        Property.NodeScope\n    );\n\n    /**\n     * Cluster-level setting specifying which node tier names are considered premium.\n     * Shards with high priority prefer allocation to premium tier nodes.\n     * Example: [\"premium\", \"hot\"]\n     */\n    public static final Setting<List<String>> CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_PREMIUM_TIERS = Setting.stringListSetting(\n        \"cluster.routing.allocation.priority.premium_tiers\",\n        java.util.List.of(\"premium\"),\n        Property.Dynamic,\n        Property.NodeScope\n    );\n\n    /**\n     * Cluster-level setting specifying the priority threshold above which\n     * to apply premium tier preferences. CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_THRESHOLD = Setting.intSetting(\n        \"cluster.routing.allocation.priority.threshold\",\n        70,\n        0,\n        100,\n        Property.Dynamic,\n        Property.NodeScope\n    );\n\n    /**\n     * Index-level setting specifying the priority of this index for shard allocation.\n     * Higher values indicate higher priority for placement on // Delegate allocator for actual shard balancing\n    private final BalancedShardsAllocator delegateAllocator;\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a new PriorityShardsAllocator with default configuration.\n     * The delegate BalancedShardsAllocator uses standard settings.\n     */\n    public PriorityShardsAllocator() {\n        this.delegateAllocator = new BalancedShardsAllocator();\n    }\n\n    /**\n cluster settings to watch for priority configuration\n     * @param delegateAllocator the wrapped allocator for balancing decisions\n     */\n    @Inject\n    public PriorityShardsAllocator(\n        ClusterSettings clusterSettings,\n        BalancedShardsAllocator delegateAllocator\n    ) {\n        this.delegateAllocator = delegateAllocator;\n\n        // Initialize settings from cluster configuration\n        this.priorityAllocationEnabled = CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_ENABLED.get(clusterSettings.getSettings());\n        this.premiumTiers = CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_PREMIUM_TIERS.get(clusterSettings.getSettings());\n        this.priorityThreshold = CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_THRESHOLD.get(clusterSettings.getSettings());\n\n        // Register listeners for dynamic updates\n        clusterSettings.addSettingsUpdateConsumer(\n            CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_ENABLED,\n            this::setPriorityAllocationEnabled\n        );\n        clusterSettings.addSettingsUpdateConsumer(\n            CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_PREMIUM_TIERS,\n            this::setPremiumTiers\n        );\n        clusterSettings.addSettingsUpdateConsumer(\n            CLUSTER_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY_THRESHOLD,\n            this::setPriorityThreshold\n        );\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Main allocation method. Sorts unassigned shards by priority and delegates\n     * to the wrapped BalancedShardsAllocator for actual allocation decisions.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * Algorithm:\n     * <ol>\n     *   <li>If priority allocation is disabled, delegate directly</li>\n     *   <li>Otherwise, sort unassigned shards by index priority (descending)</li>\n     *   <li>Invoke delegate allocator's allocate() method</li>\n     * </ol>\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param allocation the current routing allocation state\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void allocate(RoutingAllocation allocation) {\n        if (!priorityAllocationEnabled) {\n            // Feature disabled; use standard balanced allocation\n            delegateAllocator.allocate(allocation);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Sort unassigned shards by priority (highest first)\n        sortUnassignedShardsByPriority(allocation);\n\n        // Delegate to BalancedShardsAllocator for balanced shard distribution\n        delegateAllocator.allocate(allocation);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Async variant of allocate(). Delegates to the wrapped allocator's async method.\n     *\n     * @param allocation the current routing allocation state\n     * @param listener listener to be called once async allocation is complete\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void allocate(RoutingAllocation allocation, ActionListener<Void> listener) {\n        if (!priorityAllocationEnabled) {\n            delegateAllocator.allocate(allocation, listener);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        sortUnassignedShardsByPriority(allocation);\n        delegateAllocator.allocate(allocation, listener);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Executes explicit allocation commands. Delegates to the wrapped allocator.\n     *\n     * @param allocation the current routing allocation state\n     * @param commands the allocation commands to execute\n     * @param explain whether to return explain information\n     * @param retryFailed whether to reset the failed counter for retryable shards\n     * @return explanations for each executed command\n     */\n    @Override\n    public RoutingExplanations execute(\n        RoutingAllocation allocation,\n        AllocationCommands commands,\n        boolean explain,\n        boolean retryFailed\n    ) {\n        return delegateAllocator.execute(allocation, commands, explain, retryFailed);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns the allocation decision for a single shard. Indices without an explicit\n     * priority setting use the default value of 50.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * Time Complexity: O(n log n) where n = number of unassigned shards\n     * This is typically << 1000 shards in most clusters, making the overhead negligible.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param allocation the routing allocation containing the unassigned shards to sort\n     */\n    private void sortUnassignedShardsByPriority(RoutingAllocation allocation) {\n        try {\n            var unassignedShards = allocation.routingNodes().unassigned();\n            if (unassignedShards == null || unassignedShards.size() == 0) {\n                return; // No shards to sort\n            }\n\n            // Create a mutable list of shards sorted by priority (descending)\n            List<ShardRouting> shardsToSort = new ArrayList<>(unassignedShards.size());\n            for (ShardRouting shard : unassignedShards) {\n                shardsToSort.add(shard);\n            }\n\n            // Sort by index priority (descending: highest priority first)\n            shardsToSort.sort(\n                Comparator.comparingInt(\n                    (ShardRouting shard) -> getIndexPriority(allocation, shard)\n                ).reversed()\n            );\n\n            // Replace the unassigned shards iterator with sorted shards\n            // This requires calling internal routing nodes methods\n            // Note: This is pseudocode; actual implementation depends on\n            // RoutingNodes API for reordering\n            reorderUnassignedShards(allocation, shardsToSort);\n\n            if (logger.isDebugEnabled()) {\n                logger.debug(\n                    \"Sorted {} unassigned shards by priority (feature enabled)\",\n                    shardsToSort.size()\n                );\n            }\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            // Log error but don't fail allocation on sorting error\n            logger.warn(\"Failed to sort unassigned shards by priority; continuing with standard order\", e);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Reorders the unassigned shards in the routing nodes to match the priority-sorted list.\n     * This is a placeholder for the actual reordering implementation, which depends on\n     * the RoutingNodes API.\n     *\n     * @param allocation the routing allocation state\n     * @param sortedShards the shards sorted by priority (descending)\n     */\n    private void reorderUnassignedShards(RoutingAllocation allocation, List<ShardRouting> sortedShards) {\n        // TODO: Implement actual reordering using RoutingNodes API\n        // This may involve:\n        // 1. Clearing the current unassigned shards collection\n        // 2. Adding shards back in priority order\n        // OR\n        // 3. Using a custom iterator/wrapper that returns shards in priority order\n        //\n        // Example (pseudocode):\n        // RoutingNodes routingNodes = allocation.routingNodes();\n        // routingNodes.unassigned().clear();\n        // for (ShardRouting shard : sortedShards) {\n        //     routingNodes.unassigned().add(shard);\n        // }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Retrieves the priority value for an index from its metadata.\n     * Falls back to the default priority if not explicitly set.\n     *\n     * @param allocation the routing allocation state (contains cluster metadata)\n     * @param shard the shard whose index priority to retrieve\n     * @return the index priority (0-100), or default 50 if not set\n     */\n    private int getIndexPriority(RoutingAllocation allocation, ShardRouting shard) {\n        try {\n            IndexMetadata indexMetadata = allocation.metadata().getIndexSafe(shard.index());\n            // TODO: Extract priority from indexMetadata\n            // Pseudo-code:\n            // return indexMetadata.getSettings().getAsInt(\n            //     INDEX_ROUTING_ALLOCATION_PRIORITY,\n            //     50  // default priority\n            // );\n            return 50; // placeholder\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            logger.warn(\"Failed to retrieve priority for index [{}], using default\", shard.index(), e);\n            return 50; // default priority on error\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Determines if a node is classified as premium tier.\n     * Queries the node's attributes for a tier classification and checks\n     * if it matches one of the configured premium tiers.\n     *\n     * @param nodeName the name/ID of the node to check\n     * @param allocation the routing allocation state (contains node metadata)\n     * @return true if the node is classified as a premium tier node\n     */\n    private boolean isNodePremiumTier(String nodeName,   "content": "/*\n * Copyright Elasticsearch B.V. and/or licensed to Elasticsearch B.V. under one\n * or more contributor license agreements.
